 ' The attitude of Gujarat Chief Minister Narendra Modi on the former Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) organization General Secretary, Sanjay Joshi case, has now 'ignited' the Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh (RSS)
 sangh ne jahaan modi kii kaaryastylee par sawaal uthaae hai vahiin spasht shabdon main yah bhi ishaara kiya he ki sirf vahi pradhanmantri pad ke daavedaar nahin hai, kai rajyon ke mukhyamantriyon ke saath kai kendriya netaa bhi is pad kii yogyata rakhte hai
 Actually, these things are said in the latest issue of 'panchajanya'
 bhaajapa ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani ke blog evam party ke mukhpatr 'camel sandesh' ke jariye party kii maujuuda sthiti par jataai gai chita main aresas ke mukhpatr panchajnya ne ijapha kar diya he
 An article published in the latest issue of 'panchjanya' titled 'challenges before the BJP' states, "modi needs to rethink about his style of work and organizational capacity
" mumbai kii rashtriya kaaryakarini kii baithak ke samay sanjay joshi prakaran main modi kii bhoomika bahut vichaarneey he
 " gyaat ho ki bhaajapa kii rashtriya kaaryakarini kii baithak haal hi main mumbai main sampann hui
 Just before the meeting, Sanjay Joshi, a senior pracharak of the Sangh, resigned from the national executive
 yah spasht tha ki modi ke dabaav main bhaajapa ne joshi se istipha dene ke liye kaha
 It was only after Joshi's resignation that Modi attended the executive meeting
 lekh main modi ke is vyavhaar kii aalochana kii gai he
 According to the article, "we are not aware of what behavior Modi annoyed Joshi
 ham keval itnaa jaanate hai ki modi or joshi donon hi sangh ke prachaarak rahe hai
 In spite of deep reverence for the Sangh, why Modi could not resolve his displeasure with his fellow campaigner Joshi remains a puzzle
 " According to the article, "before the executive meeting, Modi made Joshi's resignation a matter of prestige and in doing so he gave an opportunity for propaganda against the Sangh and the BJP
 " After the bjp's national executive meeting, Advani has expressed his dissatisfaction over the party's activities through his blog

 a few days later, Modi's behavior was targeted in the party's mouthpiece Kamal Sandesh

3 million card details on one website

 ol india radio ke saath ek saakshaatkaar main raay ne kaha, ‘hamen or adhikaron kii jarurat nahin he

 The CAG has so much authority and so much leeway that it can carry out its audit work without hindrance

 i have never had to face any pressure while preparing the report
